This\n    95→\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n    96→\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n    97→\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n    98→\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n    99→\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n   100→\t// destination rule.\n   101→\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n   102→\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n   103→\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n   104→\t// be forwarded.\n   105→\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n   106→\n   107→\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n   108→\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n   109→\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n   110→\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n   111→\n   112→\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n   113→\t// Istio configuration.\n   114→\t//\n   115→\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n   116→\tRootNamespace string\n   117→}\n   118→\n   119→// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\n   120→func (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n   121→\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n   122→\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n   123→\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n   124→\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n   125→\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n   126→\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n   127→\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n   128→\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n   129→\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n   130→\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n   131→\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n   132→}\n   133→\n   134→// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n   135→// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n   136→// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n   137→// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\n   138→type IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n   139→\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n   140→\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n   141→\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n   142→\n   143→\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n   144→\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n   145→\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n   146→\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n   147→\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n   148→\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n   149→\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n   150→\tservices []*Service\n   151→\n   152→\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n   153→\t// As with per listener services, this\n   154→\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n   155→\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n   156→\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. We need a\n   157→\t// virtualService set per listener and not one per sidecarScope because\n   158→\t// each listener imports an independent set of virtual services.\n   159→\t// Listener 1 could import a public virtual service for serviceA from\n   160→\t// namespace A that has some path rewrite, while listener2 could import\n   161→\t// a private virtual service for serviceA from the local namespace,\n   162→\t// with a different path rewrite or no path rewrites.\n   163→\tvirtualServices []config.Config\n   164→\n   165→\tlistenerHosts map[string][]host.Name\n   166→}\n   167→\n   168→const defaultSidecar = \"default-sidecar\"\n   169→\n   170→// DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace is a sidecar scope object with a default catch all egress listener\n   171→// that matches the default Istio behavior: a sidecar has listeners for all services in the mesh\n   172→// We use this scope when the user has not set any sidecar Config for a given config namespace.\n   173→func DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n   174→\tdefaultEgressListener := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n   175→\t\tIstioListener: &networking.IstioEgressListener{\n   176→\t\t\tHosts: []string{\"*/*\"},\n   177→\t\t},\n   178→\t}\n   179→\tdefaultEgressListener.services = ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n   180→\tdefaultEgressListener.virtualServices = ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n   181→\n   182→\tout := &SidecarScope{\n   183→\t\tName:               defaultSidecar,\n   184→\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n   185→\t\tEgressListeners:    []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper{defaultEgressListener},\n   186→\t\tservices:           defaultEgressListener.services,\n   187→\t\tdestinationRules:   make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config),\n   188→\t\tservicesByHostname: make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(defaultEgressListener.services)),\n   189→\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n   190→\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n   191→\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n   192→\t}\n   193→\n   194→\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n   195→\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n   196→\t// that these services need\n   197→\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n   198→\t\t// In some scenarios, there may be multiple Services defined for the same hostname due to ServiceEntry allowing\n   199→\t\t// arbitrary hostnames. In these cases, we want to pick the first Service, which is the oldest. This ensures\n   200→\t\t// newly created Services cannot take ownership unexpectedly.\n   201→\t\t// However, the Service is from Kubernetes it should take precedence over ones not. This prevents someone from\n   202→\t\t// \"domain squatting\" on the hostname before a Kubernetes Service is created.\n   203→\t\t// This relies on the assumption that\n   204→\t\tif existing, f := out.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname]; f &&\n   205→\t\t\t!(existing.Attributes.ServiceRegistry != provider.Kubernetes && s.Attributes.ServiceRegistry == provider.Kubernetes) {\n   206→\t\t\tcontinue\n   207→\t\t}\n   208→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   209→\t\tif dr := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); dr != nil {\n   210→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = dr\n   211→\t\t}\n   212→\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   213→\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n   214→\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n   215→\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n   216→\t\t})\n   217→\t}\n   218→\n   219→\tfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n   220→\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n   221→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   222→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n   223→\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n   224→\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n   225→\t\t\t})\n   226→\t\t}\n   227→\t}\n   228→\n   229→\tfor _, el := range out.EgressListeners {\n   230→\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n   231→\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(el.virtualServices)\n   232→\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n   233→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n   234→\t\t}\n   235→\t\tfor _, vs := range el.virtualServices {\n   236→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   237→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n   238→\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n   239→\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n   240→\t\t\t})\n   241→\t\t}\n   242→\t}\n   243→\n   244→\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n   245→\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n   246→\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n   247→\t\t}\n   248→\t}\n   249→\n   250→\treturn out\n   251→}\n   252→\n   253→// ConvertToSidecarScope converts from Sidecar config to SidecarScope object\n   254→func ConvertToSidecarScope(ps *PushContext, sidecarConfig *config.Config, configNamespace string) *SidecarScope {\n   255→\tif sidecarConfig == nil {\n   256→\t\treturn DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace(ps, configNamespace)\n   257→\t}\n   258→\n   259→\tsidecar := sidecarConfig.Spec.(*networking.Sidecar)\n   260→\tout := &SidecarScope{\n   261→\t\tName:               sidecarConfig.Name,\n   262→\t\tNamespace:          configNamespace,\n   263→\t\tSidecar:            sidecar,\n   264→\t\tconfigDependencies: make(map[uint64]struct{}),\n   265→\t\tRootNamespace:      ps.Mesh.RootNamespace,\n   266→\t\tVersion:            ps.PushVersion,\n   267→\t}\n   268→\n   269→\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   270→\t\tKind:      gvk.Sidecar,\n   271→\t\tName:      sidecarConfig.Name,\n   272→\t\tNamespace: sidecarConfig.Namespace,\n   273→\t})\n   274→\n   275→\tegressConfigs := sidecar.Egress\n   276→\t// If egress not set, setup a default listener\n   277→\tif len(egressConfigs) == 0 {\n   278→\t\tegressConfigs = append(egressConfigs, &networking.IstioEgressListener{Hosts: []string{\"*/*\"}})\n   279→\t}\n   280→\tout.EgressListeners = make([]*IstioEgressListenerWrapper, 0, len(egressConfigs))\n   281→\tfor _, e := range egressConfigs {\n   282→\t\tout.EgressListeners = append(out.EgressListeners,\n   283→\t\t\tconvertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps, configNamespace, e))\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\t// Now collect all the imported services across all egress listeners in\n   287→\t// this sidecar crd. This is needed to generate CDS output\n   288→\tout.services = make([]*Service, 0)\n   289→\ttype serviceIndex struct {\n   290→\t\tsvc   *Service\n   291→\t\tindex int // index record the position of the svc in slice\n   292→\t}\n   293→\tservicesAdded := make(map[host.Name]serviceIndex)\n   294→\taddService := func(s *Service) {\n   295→\t\tif s == nil {\n   296→\t\t\treturn\n   297→\t\t}\n   298→\t\tif foundSvc, found := servicesAdded[s.Hostname]; !found {\n   299→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   300→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.ServiceEntry,\n   301→\t\t\t\tName:      string(s.Hostname),\n   302→\t\t\t\tNamespace: s.Attributes.Namespace,\n   303→\t\t\t})\n   304→\t\t\tout.services = append(out.services, s)\n   305→\t\t\tservicesAdded[s.Hostname] = serviceIndex{s, len(out.services) - 1}\n   306→\t\t} else if foundSvc.svc.Attributes.Namespace == s.Attributes.Namespace && s.Ports != nil && len(s.Ports) > 0 {\n   307→\t\t\t// merge the ports to service when each listener generates partial service\n   308→\t\t\t// we only merge if the found service is in the same namespace as the one we're trying to add\n   309→\t\t\tcopied := foundSvc.svc.DeepCopy()\n   310→\t\t\tfor _, p := range s.Ports {\n   311→\t\t\t\tfound := false\n   312→\t\t\t\tfor _, osp := range copied.Ports {\n   313→\t\t\t\t\tif p.Port == osp.Port {\n   314→\t\t\t\t\t\tfound = true\n   315→\t\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   316→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   317→\t\t\t\t}\n   318→\t\t\t\tif !found {\n   319→\t\t\t\t\tcopied.Ports = append(copied.Ports, p)\n   320→\t\t\t\t}\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t\t// replace service in slice\n   323→\t\t\tout.services[foundSvc.index] = copied\n   324→\t\t}\n   325→\t}\n   326→\n   327→\tfor _, listener := range out.EgressListeners {\n   328→\t\t// First add the explicitly requested services, which take priority\n   329→\t\tfor _, s := range listener.services {\n   330→\t\t\taddService(s)\n   331→\t\t}\n   332→\t\t// add dependencies on delegate virtual services\n   333→\t\tdelegates := ps.DelegateVirtualServicesConfigKey(listener.virtualServices)\n   334→\t\tfor _, delegate := range delegates {\n   335→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(delegate)\n   336→\t\t}\n   337→\n   338→\t\tmatchPort := needsPortMatch(listener)\n   339→\t\t// Infer more possible destinations from virtual services\n   340→\t\t// Services chosen here will not override services explicitly requested in listener.services.\n   341→\t\t// That way, if there is ambiguity around what hostname to pick, a user can specify the one they\n   342→\t\t// want in the hosts field, and the potentially random choice below won't matter\n   343→\t\tfor _, vs := range listener.virtualServices {\n   344→\t\t\tv := vs.Spec.(*networking.VirtualService)\n   345→\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   346→\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.VirtualService,\n   347→\t\t\t\tName:      vs.Name,\n   348→\t\t\t\tNamespace: vs.Namespace,\n   349→\t\t\t})\n   350→\n   351→\t\t\tfor _, h := range virtualServiceDestinationHosts(v) {\n   352→\t\t\t\t// Default to this hostname in our config namespace\n   353→\t\t\t\tif s, ok := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)][configNamespace]; ok {\n   354→\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   355→\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   356→\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   357→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(s, listener)\n   358→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   359→\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = s\n   360→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   361→\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n   362→\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n   363→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   364→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   365→\n   366→\t\t\t\t\t// We couldn't find the hostname in our config namespace\n   367→\t\t\t\t\t// We have to pick one arbitrarily for now, so we'll pick the first namespace alphabetically\n   368→\t\t\t\t\t// TODO: could we choose services more intelligently based on their ports?\n   369→\t\t\t\t\tbyNamespace := ps.ServiceIndex.HostnameAndNamespace[host.Name(h)]\n   370→\t\t\t\t\tif len(byNamespace) == 0 {\n   371→\t\t\t\t\t\t// This hostname isn't found anywhere\n   372→\t\t\t\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Could not find service hostname %s parsed from %s\", h, vs.Key())\n   373→\t\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   374→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t\t\t\t\tns := make([]string, 0, len(byNamespace))\n   377→\t\t\t\t\tfor k := range byNamespace {\n   378→\t\t\t\t\t\tif ps.IsServiceVisible(byNamespace[k], configNamespace) {\n   379→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tns = append(ns, k)\n   380→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   381→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   382→\t\t\t\t\tif len(ns) > 0 {\n   383→\t\t\t\t\t\tsort.Strings(ns)\n   384→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Pick first namespace alphabetically\n   385→\t\t\t\t\t\t// This won't overwrite hostnames that have already been found eg because they were requested in hosts\n   386→\t\t\t\t\t\tvar vss *Service\n   387→\t\t\t\t\t\tif matchPort {\n   388→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = serviceMatchingListenerPort(byNamespace[ns[0]], listener)\n   389→\t\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   390→\t\t\t\t\t\t\tvss = byNamespace[ns[0]]\n   391→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   392→\t\t\t\t\t\tif vss != nil {\n   393→\t\t\t\t\t\t\taddService(vss)\n   394→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   395→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   396→\t\t\t\t}\n   397→\t\t\t}\n   398→\t\t}\n   399→\t}\n   400→\n   401→\t// Now that we have all the services that sidecars using this scope (in\n   402→\t// this config namespace) will see, identify all the destinationRules\n   403→\t// that these services need\n   404→\tout.servicesByHostname = make(map[host.Name]*Service, len(out.services))\n   405→\tout.destinationRules = make(map[host.Name][]*config.Config)\n   406→\tfor _, s := range out.services {\n   407→\t\tout.servicesByHostname[s.Hostname] = s\n   408→\t\tif drList := ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s); drList != nil {\n   409→\t\t\tout.destinationRules[s.Hostname] = drList\n   410→\t\t\tfor _, dr := range drList {\n   411→\t\t\t\tout.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n   412→\t\t\t\t\tKind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n   413→\t\t\t\t\tName:      dr.Name,\n   414→\t\t\t\t\tNamespace: dr.Namespace,\n   415→\t\t\t\t})\n   416→\t\t\t}\n   417→\t\t}\n   418→\t}\n   419→\n   420→\tif sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy == nil {\n   421→\t\tif ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy != nil {\n   422→\t\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = &networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy{\n   423→\t\t\t\tMode: networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy_Mode(ps.Mesh.OutboundTrafficPolicy.Mode),\n   424→\t\t\t}\n   425→\t\t}\n   426→\t} else {\n   427→\t\tout.OutboundTrafficPolicy = sidecar.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n   428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\treturn out\n   431→}\n   432→\n   433→func convertIstioListenerToWrapper(ps *PushContext, configNamespace string,\n   434→\tistioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   435→\tout := &IstioEgressListenerWrapper{\n   436→\t\tIstioListener: istioListener,\n   437→\t}\n   438→\n   439→\tout.listenerHosts = make(map[string][]host.Name)\n   440→\tfor _, h := range istioListener.Hosts {\n   441→\t\tparts := strings.SplitN(h, \"/\", 2)\n   442→\t\tif len(parts) < 2 {\n   443→\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"Illegal host in sidecar resource: %s, host must be of form namespace/dnsName\", h)\n   444→\t\t\tcontinue\n   445→\t\t}\n   446→\t\tif parts[0] == currentNamespace {\n   447→\t\t\tparts[0] = configNamespace\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\t\tif _, exists := out.listenerHosts[parts[0]]; !exists {\n   450→\t\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = make([]host.Name, 0)\n   451→\t\t}\n   452→\t\tout.listenerHosts[parts[0]] = append(out.listenerHosts[parts[0]], host.Name(parts[1]))\n   453→\t}\n   454→\n   455→\tvses := ps.VirtualServicesForGateway(configNamespace, constants.IstioMeshGateway)\n   456→\tout.virtualServices = SelectVirtualServices(vses, out.listenerHosts)\n   457→\tsvces := ps.servicesExportedToNamespace(configNamespace)\n   458→\tout.services = out.selectServices(svces, configNamespace, out.listenerHosts)\n   459→\n   460→\treturn out\n   461→}\n   462→\n   463→// GetEgressListenerForRDS returns the egress listener corresponding to\n   464→// the listener port or the bind address or the catch all listener\n   465→func (sc *SidecarScope) GetEgressListenerForRDS(port int, bind string) *IstioEgressListenerWrapper {\n   466→\tif sc == nil {\n   467→\t\treturn nil\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\tfor _, e := range sc.EgressListeners {\n   471→\t\t// We hit a catchall listener. This is the last listener in the list of listeners\n   472→\t\t// return as is\n   473→\t\tif e.IstioListener == nil || e.IstioListener.Port == nil {\n   474→\t\t\treturn e\n   475→\t\t}\n   476→\n   477→\t\t// Check if the ports match\n   478→\t\t// for unix domain sockets (i.e. port == 0), check if the bind is equal to the routeName\n   479→\t\tif int(e.IstioListener.Port.Number) == port {\n   480→\t\t\tif port == 0 { // unix domain socket\n   481→\t\t\t\tif e.IstioListener.Bind == bind {\n   482→\t\t\t\t\treturn e\n   483→\t\t\t\t}\n   484→\t\t\t\t// no match.. continue searching\n   485→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   486→\t\t\t}\n   487→\t\t\t// this is a non-zero port match\n   488→\t\t\treturn e\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t}\n   491→\n   492→\t// This should never be reached unless user explicitly set an empty array for egress\n   493→\t// listeners which we actually forbid\n   494→\treturn nil\n   495→}\n   496→\n   497→// HasIngressListener returns if the sidecar scope has ingress listener set\n   498→func (sc *SidecarScope) HasIngressListener() bool {\n   499→\tif sc == nil {\n   500→\t\treturn false\n   501→\t}\n   502→\n   503→\tif sc.Sidecar == nil || len(sc.Sidecar.Ingress) == 0 {\n   504→\t\treturn false\n   505→\t}\n   506→\n   507→\treturn true\n   508→}\n   509→\n   510→// Services returns the list of services imported by this egress listener\n   511→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) Services() []*Service {\n   512→\treturn ilw.services\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→// VirtualServices returns the list of virtual services imported by this\n   516→// egress listener\n   517→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) VirtualServices() []config.Config {\n   518→\treturn ilw.virtualServices\n   519→}\n   520→\n   521→// DependsOnConfig determines if the proxy depends on the given config.\n   522→// Returns whether depends on this config or this kind of config is not scoped(unknown to be depended) here.\n   523→func (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n   524→\tif sc == nil {\n   525→\t\treturn true\n   526→\t}\n   527→\n   528→\t// This kind of config will trigger a change if made in the root namespace or the same namespace\n   529→\tif _, f := clusterScopedConfigTypes[config.Kind]; f {\n   530→\t\treturn config.Namespace == sc.RootNamespace || config.Namespace == sc.Namespace\n   531→\t}\n   532→\n   533→\t// This kind of config is unknown to sidecarScope.\n   534→\tif _, f := sidecarScopeKnownConfigTypes[config.Kind]; !f {\n   535→\t\treturn true\n   536→\t}\n   537→\n   538→\t_, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n   539→\treturn exists\n   540→}\n   541→\n   542→// AddConfigDependencies add extra config dependencies to this scope. This action should be done before the\n   543→// SidecarScope being used to avoid concurrent read/write.\n   544→func (sc *SidecarScope) AddConfigDependencies(dependencies ...ConfigKey) {\n   545→\tif sc == nil {\n   546→\t\treturn\n   547→\t}\n   548→\tif sc.configDependencies == nil {\n   549→\t\tsc.configDependencies = make(map[uint64]struct{})\n   550→\t}\n   551→\n   552→\tfor _, config := range dependencies {\n   553→\t\tsc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()] = struct{}{}\n   554→\t}\n   555→}\n   556→\n   557→// DestinationRule returns a destinationrule for a svc.\n   558→func (sc *SidecarScope) DestinationRule(direction TrafficDirection, proxy *Proxy, svc host.Name) *config.Config {\n   559→\tdestinationRules := sc.destinationRules[svc]\n   560→\tvar catchAllDr *config.Config\n   561→\tfor _, destRule := range destinationRules {\n   562→\t\tdestinationRule := destRule.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n   563→\t\tif destinationRule.GetWorkloadSelector() == nil {\n   564→\t\t\tcatchAllDr = destRule\n   565→\t\t}\n   566→\t\t// filter DestinationRule based on workloadSelector for outbound configs.\n   567→\t\t// WorkloadSelector configuration is honored portion of the Sidecar config.\n   592→// Note that the returned service could be trimmed.\n   593→func (ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) selectServices(services []*Service, configNamespace string, hosts map[string][]host.Name) []*Service {\n   594→\timportedServices := make([]*Service, 0)\n   595→\twildcardHosts, wnsFound := hosts[wildcardNamespace]\n   596→\tfor _, s := range services {\n 630→}\n   631→\n   632→// Return the original service or a trimmed service which has a subset of the ports in original service.\n   633→func matchingService(importedHosts []host.Name, service 641→\t\t\treturn service\n   642→\t\t}\n   643→\t}\n   644→\treturn nil\n   645→}\n   646→\n   647→// serviceMatchingListenerPort constructs service with listener port.\n   648→func 657→}\n   658→\n   659→func needsPortMatch(ilw *IstioEgressListenerWrapper) bool {\n   660→\t// If a listener is defined with a port, we should match services with port except in the following case.\n   661→\t//  - If Port's protocol is proxy protocol(HTTP_PROXY) in which case the egress listener is used as generic egress http proxy.\n   662→\treturn ilw.IstioListener != nil && Sidecar resource with some\n// preprocessed data to determine the list of services, virtualServices,\n// and destinationRules that are accessible to a given\n// sidecar. Precomputing the list of services, virtual services, dest rules\n// for a sidecar improves performance as we no longer need to compute this\n// list for every sidecar. We simply have to match a sidecar to a\n// SidecarScope. Note that this is not the same as public/private scoped\n// services. The list of services seen by every sidecar scope (namespace\n// wide or per workload) depends on the imports, the listeners, and other\n// settings.\n//\n// Every proxy workload of SidecarProxy type will always map to a\n// SidecarScope object. If the proxy's namespace does not have a user\n// specified Sidecar CRD, we will construct one that has a catch all egress\n// listener that imports every public service/virtualService in the mesh.\ntype SidecarScope struct {\n\tName string\n\t// This is the namespace where the sidecar takes effect,\n\t// maybe different from the ns where sidecar resides if sidecar is in root ns.\n\tNamespace string\n\t// The crd itself. Can be nil if we are constructing the default\n\t// sidecar scope\n\tSidecar *networking.Sidecar\n\n\t// Version this sidecar was computed for\n\tVersion string\n\n\t// Set of egress listeners, and their associated services.  A sidecar\n\t// scope should have either ingress/egress listeners or both.  For\n\t// every proxy workload that maps to a sidecar API object (or the\n\t// default object), we will go through every egress listener in the\n\t// object and process the Envoy listener or RDS based on the imported\n\t// services/virtual services in that listener.\n\tEgressListeners []*IstioEgressListenerWrapper\n\n\t// Union of services imported across all egress listeners for use by CDS code.\n\tservices           []*Service\n\tservicesByHostname map[host.Name]*Service\n\n\t// Destination rules imported across all egress listeners. This\n\t// contains the computed set based on public/private destination rules\n\t// as well as the inherited ones, in addition to the wildcard matches\n\t// such as *.com applying to foo.bar.com. Each hostname in this map\n\t// corresponds to a service in the services array above. When computing\n\t// CDS, we simply have to find the matching service and return the\n\t// destination rule.\n\tdestinationRules map[host.Name][]*config.Config\n\t// OutboundTrafficPolicy defines the outbound traffic policy for this sidecar.\n\t// If OutboundTrafficPolicy is ALLOW_ANY traffic to unknown destinations will\n\t// be forwarded.\n\tOutboundTrafficPolicy *networking.OutboundTrafficPolicy\n\n\t// Set of known configs this sidecar depends on.\n\t// This field will be used to determine the config/resource scope\n\t// which means which config changes will affect the proxies within this scope.\n\tconfigDependencies map[uint64]struct{}\n\n\t// The namespace to treat as the administrative root namespace for\n\t// Istio configuration.\n\t//\n\t// Changes to Sidecar resources in this namespace will trigger a push.\n\tRootNamespace string\n}\n\n// MarshalJSON implements json.Marshaller\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {\n\t// Json cannot expose unexported fields, so copy the ones we want here\n\treturn json.MarshalIndent(map[string]interface{}{\n\t\t\"version\":               sc.Version,\n\t\t\"rootNamespace\":         sc.RootNamespace,\n\t\t\"name\":                  sc.Name,\n\t\t\"namespace\":             sc.Namespace,\n\t\t\"outboundTrafficPolicy\": sc.OutboundTrafficPolicy,\n\t\t\"services\":              sc.services,\n\t\t\"sidecar\":               sc.Sidecar,\n\t\t\"destinationRules\":      sc.destinationRules,\n\t}, \"\", \"  \")\n}\n\n// IstioEgressListenerWrapper is a wrapper for\n// networking.IstioEgressListener object. The wrapper provides performance\n// optimizations as it allows us to precompute and store the list of\n// services/virtualServices that apply to this listener.\ntype IstioEgressListenerWrapper struct {\n\t// The actual IstioEgressListener api object from the Config. It can be\n\t// nil if this is for the default sidecar scope.\n\tIstioListener *networking.IstioEgressListener\n\n\t// List of services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// This will be used by LDS and RDS code when\n\t// building the set of virtual hosts or the tcp filterchain matches for\n\t// a given listener port. Two listeners, on user specified ports or\n\t// unix domain sockets could have completely different sets of\n\t// services. So a global list of services per sidecar scope will be\n\t// incorrect. Hence the per listener set of services.\n\tservices []*Service\n\n\t// List of virtual services imported by this egress listener above.\n\t// As with per listener services, this\n\t// will be used by RDS code to compute the virtual host configs for\n\t// http listeners, as well as by TCP/TLS filter code to compute the\n\t// service routing configs and the filter chain matches. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01KjBqv5FBxC8LzMh3cnc9VG","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Perfect! Now I can see the issue clearly. Let me trace through the logic:\n\n1. When a DestinationRule is updated in Kubernetes, a ConfigUpdate is triggered\n2. The ConfigUpdate creates a ConfigKey with the DR's name and namespace\n3. This ConfigKey is added to req.ConfigsUpdated\n4. For each proxy, ConfigAffectsProxy is called with the updated ConfigKey\n5. ConfigAffectsProxy calls checkProxyDependencies for SidecarProxy\n6. checkProxyDependencies calls proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)\n7. DependsOnConfig looks up the configKey's hash in sc.configDependencies\n\nThe problem is:\n- When two DestinationRules for the same host are merged in mergeDestinationRule(), only one DR's name/namespace is retained as the ConfigKey\n- The other DR's metadata is lost in the merged result\n- When the lost DR is updated in Kubernetes, a ConfigKey is generated with that DR's name/namespace\n- DependsOnConfig is called with this ConfigKey\n- But this ConfigKey is not in sc.configDependencies because only the retained DR's ConfigKey was added\n- So DependsOnConfig returns false and the push is skipped\n\nNow let me look at what gets added to configDependencies in AddConfigDependencies in sidecar.go. I can see in the sidecar.go file that:\n\nLines 219-226 show:\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAnd similarly in ConvertToSidecarScope at lines 410-416:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,\n    })\n}\n```\n\nThe issue is that `dr.Name` and `dr.Namespace` come from the config.Config object returned by destinationRule(), which only contains the metadata of ONE of the merged DRs (the last one that was merged). When the merging logic in destination_rule.go combines multiple DestinationRules for the same host, it preserves only the final DR's identity while discarding the others, so only that single ConfigKey gets registered as a dependency.\n\nLooking at the mergeDestinationRule function, it takes a consolidatedDestRules map of hosts to DR lists and for each host with existing rules, it deep copies the current rule and updates it with subsets and traffic policy from incoming rules before storing it back. New incoming rules that don't match existing ones get appended. This means each host in consolidatedDestRules maintains its own config.Config with its own metadata, but when we later extract the dependency, we're only capturing the metadata from whichever DR object we happen to be working with at that moment. the system doesn't detect it as a dependency change because its name/namespace aren't tracked. When AddConfigDependencies processes the consolidated rule, it only registers the first DR's identity, so updates to other merged DRs go unnoticed. The fundamental issue is that merging multiple DRs into a single consolidated object causes metadata loss—only the winning DR's name and namespace survive, while the others' identities disappear from the dependency tracking system.\n\nTo resolve this, I need to preserve all contributing DR identities. Options include storing a list of all merged DR metadata in the consolidated structure, registering dependencies for each contributor when building the SidecarScope, or avoiding the merge entirely and handling multiple DRs per host separately. I should examine the AddConfigDependencies implementation more closely and check if DRs are processed elsewhere in the {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_016vFcpSBKvkRxBzWgfB5XKv","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_012fAHLQdbsPauFiG4QEmdis","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/logs/agent/investigation.md","content":"# Investigation Report: Stale Envoy Route Configuration After DestinationRule Update in Istio\n\n## Summary\n\nWhen multiple DestinationRules (DRs) for the same host are merged during PushContext initialization, only the metadata (name/namespace) of the first merged DR is retained in the consolidated configuration. When a different contributing DR is updated, its ConfigKey fails to match the registered dependency, causing `DependsOnConfig()` to return false and the xDS push to be incorrectly skipped, leaving Envoy sidecars with stale configuration.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause spans two interacting mechanisms in the PushContext and SidecarScope layers:\n\n### 1. **Identity Loss During Merging** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`, `mergeDestinationRule()`)\n\nWhen `mergeDestinationRule()` processes multiple DestinationRules for the same host:\n- If a DR for a given host already exists in `consolidatedDestRules[host]`, the function deep copies the **existing** DR and merges the incoming DR's subsets and traffic policies **into** it\n- The merged result retains only the existing DR's `config.Config` metadata (name, namespace, creation timestamp)\n- Contributing DRs whose metadata is not retained lose their identity in the consolidated structure\n- The `consolidatedDestRules` structure contains only a single `[]*config.Config` list per hostname, not a per-DR tracking of contributors\n\n**Relevant code** (`destination_rule.go:38-109`):\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, exportToMap map[visibility.Instance]bool) {\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // ... selector matching logic ...\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy EXISTING rule\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied  // Update with merged content\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // Merge subsets from incoming rule into the copied existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n            // ... traffic policy merge ...\n        }\n    }\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe problem: After merging, `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` contains config.Config objects, but their metadata reflects only some of the contributing DRs, not all.\n\n### 2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`, `AddConfigDependencies()`)\n\nWhen a SidecarScope is built, `AddConfigDependencies()` registers config dependencies based on the DRs returned by `ps.destinationRule()`:\n\n**Relevant code** (`sidecar.go:219-227` in `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()`):\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,              // <-- Metadata from merged DR\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,          // <-- May not include all contributors\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAnd similarly at `sidecar.go:410-416` in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,                  // <-- Only the \"winning\" DR's name\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,              // <-- Only the \"winning\" DR's namespace\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**The issue**: `drList` comes from `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)`, which returns the merged configuration from `consolidatedDestRules`. Each config.Config in this list was created by merging multiple original DRs, but only retains one DR's metadata.\n\n### 3. **Push Filter Failure** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`, `checkProxyDependencies()`)\n\nWhen a DestinationRule is updated in Kubernetes:\n\n**Relevant code** (`proxy_dependencies.go:60-74`):\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false\n}\n```\n\nThis calls `DependsOnConfig()` in `sidecar.go:521-540`:\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    // ...\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists\n}\n```\n\n**The problem**:\n- When DR2 (reviews-subsets) is updated, a ConfigKey `{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}` is created\n- This ConfigKey's hash is looked up in `sc.configDependencies`\n- But `sc.configDependencies` only contains the hash of DR1's ConfigKey (because DR1's metadata was retained during merging)\n- The lookup fails, and `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`\n- The proxy is not marked as needing a push\n\n### 4. **Metadata Resolution in Networking Layers** (`pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/cluster_builder.go`)\n\nThe networking layer builds caches that reference the DR metadata:\n\n**Relevant code** (`cluster_builder.go`, `DependentConfigs()`):\n```go\nfunc (t clusterCache) DependentConfigs() []model.ConfigKey {\n    configs := []model.ConfigKey{}\n    if t.destinationRule != nil {\n        configs = append(configs, model.ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      t.destinationRule.Name,      // <-- Only one DR's name\n            Namespace: t.destinationRule.Namespace, // <-- Only one DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n    // ...\n    return configs\n}\n```\n\nThis creates a cache dependency on the DR whose metadata is retained. Updates to other DRs that contributed to the merge are not tracked.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### File References with Line Numbers\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`** - `mergeDestinationRule()` function where merged DR loses contributing DR metadata\n   - Line 65: `copied := mdr.DeepCopy()` - Only existing DR is deep copied\n   - Line 67: `mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)` - Merged result uses existing metadata\n\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:251-256`** - `consolidatedDestRules` structure definition\n   - Stores map from hostname to list of `[]*config.Config`\n   - No tracking of contributing DRs per config\n\n3. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:1672-1744`** - `SetDestinationRules()` where merging is orchestrated\n   - Line 1716: `ps.mergeDestinationRule(namespaceLocalDestRules[configs[i].Namespace], configs[i], exportToMap)` - Merges multiple DRs for same host\n\n4. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:219-227`** (DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace) and **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:410-416`** (ConvertToSidecarScope)\n   - Lines that register dependencies only from the returned merged DRs\n   - Lost DRs' ConfigKeys are never added\n\n5. **`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go:521-540`** - `DependsOnConfig()` method\n   - Line 538: `_, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]` - Looks up config hash\n   - Returns `false` if the hash is not found\n\n6. **`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go:60-74`** - `checkProxyDependencies()` and `ConfigAffectsProxy()`\n   - Line 64: `if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)` - Uses DependsOnConfig to filter pushes\n   - Line 52: `if affected && checkProxyDependencies(proxy, config)` - Returns true only if dependency exists\n\n7. **`pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/cluster_builder.go`, `DependentConfigs()`** - Builds ConfigKeys from DR metadata\n   - Creates dependency only on the DR whose metadata is retained during merging\n\n## Affected Components\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/`**\n   - `destination_rule.go` - Merges DRs, losing metadata\n   - `sidecar.go` - Registers incomplete dependencies\n   - `push_context.go` - Stores consolidated DRs without tracking contributors\n\n2. **`pilot/pkg/xds/`**\n   - `proxy_dependencies.go` - Filters pushes based on incomplete dependency check\n\n3. **`pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/`**\n   - `cluster_builder.go` - Builds ConfigKeys from incomplete DR metadata\n   - `route/route_cache.go` - Similar dependency tracking issue\n\n4. **`pilot/pkg/config/`**\n   - Config change events trigger PushRequests with ConfigKeys that don't match registered dependencies\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Updating a DestinationRule fails to trigger xDS push to Envoy sidecars; configuration remains stale\n\n2. → **Intermediate: PushRequest generated but push filtered out**\n   - When `reviews-subsets` DR is updated in Kubernetes, a config change event creates `PushRequest{ConfigsUpdated: {ConfigKey{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}}}`\n   - This PushRequest reaches `ConfigAffectsProxy()`\n\n3. → **Intermediate: DependsOnConfig returns false**\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` calls `proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config)`\n   - `config` is `ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}`\n   - `sc.configDependencies` only contains the hash of `ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-traffic-policy\", Namespace: \"default\"}`\n   - Lookup fails; `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`\n\n4. → **Intermediate: Proxy not marked for push**\n   - `checkProxyDependencies()` returns `false`\n   - Proxy is not added to the set of proxies needing update\n\n5. → **Intermediate: SidecarScope has incomplete dependencies**\n   - When `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()` or `ConvertToSidecarScope()` builds the SidecarScope:\n   - It calls `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)` which returns the merged DRs\n   - Each merged DR only has metadata from one of the contributing DRs\n   - `AddConfigDependencies()` only registers the \"winning\" DR's ConfigKey\n\n6. → **Root Cause: Only \"winning\" DR's metadata retained during merge**\n   - In `mergeDestinationRule()`, when multiple DRs exist for the same host:\n   - The function deep copies the **existing** (first) DR\n   - Merges the incoming DR's subsets/policies into the copy\n   - The merged result in `consolidatedDestRules[host]` has only the first DR's metadata\n   - Return a full list of all DRs per hostname instead of merging them\n   - Merge subsets/policies at generation time instead of storage time\n   - More memory usage but no identity loss\n   - Requires changes throughout the CDS/RDS generation pipeline\n\n3. **Option C: Use DR Host Instead of Name/Namespace**\n   - When a different contributing DR is updated, its ConfigKey fails to match the registered dependency, causing `DependsOnConfig()` to return false and the xDS push to be incorrectly skipped, leaving Envoy sidecars with stale configuration.\n\n## Root Cause\n\nThe root cause spans two interacting mechanisms in the PushContext and SidecarScope layers:\n\n### 1. **Identity Loss During Merging** (`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go`, `mergeDestinationRule()`)\n\nWhen `mergeDestinationRule()` processes multiple DestinationRules for the same host:\n- If a DR for a given host already exists in `consolidatedDestRules[host]`, the function deep copies the **existing** DR and merges the incoming DR's subsets and traffic policies **into** it\n- The merged result retains only the existing DR's `config.Config` metadata (name, namespace, creation timestamp)\n- Contributing DRs whose metadata is not retained lose their identity in the consolidated structure\n- The `consolidatedDestRules` structure contains only a single `[]*config.Config` list per hostname, not a per-DR tracking of contributors\n\n**Relevant code** (`destination_rule.go:38-109`):\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) mergeDestinationRule(p *consolidatedDestRules, destRuleConfig config.Config, exportToMap map[visibility.Instance]bool) {\n    if mdrList, exists := p.destRules[resolvedHost]; exists {\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // ... selector matching logic ...\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy EXISTING rule\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied  // Update with merged content\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // Merge subsets from incoming rule into the copied existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n            // ... traffic policy merge ...\n        }\n    }\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe problem: After merging, `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` contains config.Config objects, but their metadata reflects only some of the contributing DRs, not all.\n\n### 2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`, `AddConfigDependencies()`)\n\nWhen a SidecarScope is built, `AddConfigDependencies()` registers config dependencies based on the DRs returned by `ps.destinationRule()`:\n\n**Relevant code** (`sidecar.go:219-227` in `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()`):\n```go\nfor _, drList := range out.destinationRules {\n    for _, dr := range drList {\n        out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      dr.Name,              // <-- Metadata from merged DR\n            Namespace: dr.Namespace,          // <-- May not include all contributors\n        })\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAnd similarly at `sidecar.go:410-416` in `ConvertToSidecarScope()`:\n```go\nfor _, dr := range drList {\n    out.AddConfigDependencies(ConfigKey{\n        Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n        Name:      dr.Name,                  // <-- Only the \"winning\" DR's name\n        Namespace: dr.Namespace,              // <-- Only the \"winning\" DR's namespace\n    })\n}\n```\n\n**The issue**: `drList` comes from `ps.destinationRule(configNamespace, s)`, which returns the merged configuration from `consolidatedDestRules`. Each config.Config in this list was created by merging multiple original DRs, but only retains one DR's metadata.\n\n### 3. **Push Filter Failure** (`pilot/pkg/xds/proxy_dependencies.go`, `checkProxyDependencies()`)\n\nWhen a DestinationRule is updated in Kubernetes:\n\n**Relevant code** (`proxy_dependencies.go:60-74`):\n```go\nfunc checkProxyDependencies(proxy *model.Proxy, config model.ConfigKey) bool {\n    switch proxy.Type {\n    case model.SidecarProxy:\n        if proxy.SidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        } else if proxy.PrevSidecarScope != nil && proxy.PrevSidecarScope.DependsOnConfig(config) {\n            return true\n        }\n    }\n    return false\n}\n```\n\nThis calls `DependsOnConfig()` in `sidecar.go:521-540`:\n```go\nfunc (sc *SidecarScope) DependsOnConfig(config ConfigKey) bool {\n    // ...\n    _, exists := sc.configDependencies[config.HashCode()]\n    return exists\n}\n```\n\n**The problem**:\n- When DR2 (reviews-subsets) is updated, a ConfigKey `{Kind: DestinationRule, Name: \"reviews-subsets\", Namespace: \"default\"}` is created\n- This ConfigKey's hash is looked up in `sc.configDependencies`\n- But `sc.configDependencies` only contains the hash of DR1's ConfigKey (because DR1's metadata was retained during merging)\n- The lookup fails, and `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`\n- The proxy is not marked as needing a push\n\n### 4. **Metadata Resolution in Networking Layers** (`pilot/pkg/networking/core/v1alpha3/cluster_builder.go`)\n\nThe networking layer builds caches that reference the DR metadata:\n\n**Relevant code** (`cluster_builder.go`, `DependentConfigs()`):\n```go\nfunc (t clusterCache) DependentConfigs() []model.ConfigKey {\n    configs := []model.ConfigKey{}\n    if t.destinationRule != nil {\n        configs = append(configs, model.ConfigKey{\n            Kind:      gvk.DestinationRule,\n            Name:      t.destinationRule.Name,      // <-- Only one DR's name\n            Namespace: t.destinationRule.Namespace, // <-- Only one DR's namespace\n        })\n    }\n    // ...\n    return configs\n}\n```\n\nThis creates a cache dependency on the DR whose metadata is retained. Updates to other DRs that contributed to the merge are not tracked.\n\n## Evidence\n\n### File References with Line Numbers\n\n1. **`pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go:38-109`** - `mergeDestinationRule()` function where merged DR loses contributing DR metadata\n   - Line 65: `copied := mdr.DeepCopy()` - Only existing DR is deep copied\n   - Line 67: `mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)` - Merged result uses existing metadata\n\n2. **`pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go:251-256`** - Similar dependency tracking issue\n\n4. **`pilot/pkg/config/`**\n   - Config change events trigger PushRequests with ConfigKeys that don't match registered dependencies\n\n## Causal Chain\n\n1. **Symptom**: Updating a DestinationRule fails to trigger xDS push to Envoy sidecars; configuration remains stale\n\n2. → **Intermediate: PushRequest generated but push filtered out**\n   - `sc.configDependencies` only contains the hash of `ConfigKey{Name: \"reviews-traffic-policy\", Namespace: \"default\"}`\n   - Lookup fails; `DependsOnConfig()` returns `false`\n\n4. → **Intermediate: Proxy not marked for push**\n   - exists {\n        for i, mdr := range mdrList {\n            existingRule := mdr.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // ... selector matching logic ...\n            copied := mdr.DeepCopy()  // Deep copy EXISTING rule\n            p.destRules[resolvedHost][i] = &copied  // Update with merged content\n            mergedRule := copied.Spec.(*networking.DestinationRule)\n            // Merge subsets from incoming rule into the copied existing rule\n            for _, subset := range rule.Subsets {\n                if _, ok := existingSubset[subset.Name]; !ok {\n                    mergedRule.Subsets = append(mergedRule.Subsets, subset)\n                }\n            }\n            // ... traffic policy merge ...\n        }\n    }\n    if addRuleToProcessedDestRules {\n        p.destRules[resolvedHost] = append(p.destRules[resolvedHost], &destRuleConfig)\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThe problem: After merging, `p.destRules[resolvedHost]` contains config.Config objects, but their metadata reflects only some of the contributing DRs, not all.\n\n### 2. **Incomplete Dependency Registration** (`pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go`, `AddConfigDependencies()`)\n\nWhen a SidecarScope is built, `AddConfigDependencies()` registers config dependencies based on the DRs returned by `ps.destinationRule()`:\n\n**Relevant code** (`sidecar.go:219-227` in `DefaultSidecarScopeForNamespace()`):","numLines":50,"startLine":1,"totalLines":254}}}
